             <h3>
              About
             </h3>
             <p>

               <div class="cq-dd-paragraph">
                <div class="leadingPar-1 parsys">
                 <div class="section text">
                  <h2>
                   <span class="white-text">
                    Viewpoints
                   </span>
                  </h2>
                 </div>
                 <div class="section text">
                  <p>
                   <span class="white-text medium">
                    Point-of-care diagnostics is a growing and dynamic industry helping to improve clinical and economic outcomes globally. Abbott brings you a variety of expert viewpoints on new innovations, insights, and impacts that are shaping the future of diagnostics around the world.
                   </span>
                  </p>

                     <div class="blockPar parsys">
                      <div class="articleItem section">
                       <div class="imgWrapper">
                        <img alt="Bringing “Health on Wheels” to At-risk Teens in Cape Town" class="lazy" data-src="/content/dam/web/alere-com/viewpoints/Viewpoint-Health-on-Wheels-Article_Grid_img_384x180.jpg" role="presentation" src="/etc/designs/alere/default/images/lightbox/loading.gif"/>
                       </div>
                       <div class="contentWrapper">
                        <div class="heading">
                         <h4 class="impact">
                          Impact
                         </h4>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text">

            <div class="leadingParsys">
             <div class="parsys">
              <div class="section text">
               <h2>
                <span class="white-text">
                 Viewpoints
                </span>
               </h2>
              </div>
              <div class="section text">
               <p>
                <span class="white-text medium">
                 Point-of-care diagnostics is a growing and dynamic industry helping to improve clinical and economic outcomes globally. Abbott brings you a variety of expert viewpoints on new innovations, insights, and impacts that are shaping the future of diagnostics around the world.
                </span>
               </p>
              </div>

                  <div class="blockPar parsys">
                   <div class="articleItem section">
                    <div class="imgWrapper">
                     <img alt="Bringing “Health on Wheels” to At-risk Teens in Cape Town" class="lazy" data-src="/content/dam/web/alere-com/viewpoints/Viewpoint-Health-on-Wheels-Article_Grid_img_384x180.jpg" role="presentation" src="/etc/designs/alere/default/images/lightbox/loading.gif"/>
                    </div>
                    <div class="contentWrapper">
                     <div class="heading">
                      <h4 class="impact">
